- The provided working directory is the only submission surface for this evaluation.
- Do not `git clone`, `git init`, or fetch the target repository into the working directory or any of its subdirectories.
- Use MCP to inspect remote code, then create or edit only the files you need directly in the working directory using repository-relative paths.
- The verifier only reads changes from the provided working directory, not from any self-cloned checkout.

## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Task: Generate Javadoc for Kafka Record Batch Serialization

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/kafka--e678b4b (mirror of apache/kafka)
**Output:** Write your summary to `/workspace/documentation.md`; edit source files directly

## Objective

Generate Javadoc comments for Kafka's record batch serialization classes in `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/record/`. These classes handle the binary encoding of Kafka message batches and are critical for correctness and performance.

## Scope

Document the following classes:
- `RecordBatch` — interface defining a batch of records
- `DefaultRecordBatch` — concrete implementation of a magic v2 batch
- `MemoryRecords` — in-memory collection of record batches

For each class, document:
- Class-level Javadoc: purpose, role in the Kafka protocol, thread-safety guarantee
- Key public methods: `@param`, `@return`, `@throws` tags
- Performance characteristics where relevant (e.g., lazy decoding, copy-on-write)
- Cross-references using `{@link}` to related classes

## Quality Bar

- Thread-safety must be explicitly stated for every class (thread-safe, not thread-safe, or conditionally thread-safe)
- Performance implications must be noted for serialization/deserialization methods
- Do not add Javadoc to private methods
- Use standard Javadoc tags: `@param`, `@return`, `@throws`, `@see`, `{@link}`

## Anti-Requirements

- Do not change implementation logic
- Do not document internal/private fields

This\\n95:      * may be smaller than what is returned by {@link #sizeInBytes()}.\\n96:      * @return The number of valid bytes\\n97:      */\\n98:     public int validBytes() {\\n99:         if (validBytes >= 0)\\n100:             return validBytes;\\n101: \\n102:         int bytes = 0;\\n103:         for (RecordBatch batch : batches())\\n104:             bytes += batch.sizeInBytes();\\n105: \\n106:         this.validBytes = bytes;\\n107:         return bytes;\\n108:     }\\n109: \\n110:     @Override\\n111:     public AbstractIterator<MutableRecordBatch> batchIterator() {\\n112:         return new RecordBatchIterator<>(new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer.duplicate(), Integer.MAX_VALUE));\\n113:     }\\n114: \\n115:     /**\\n116:      * Validates the header of the first batch and returns batch size.\\n117:      * @return first batch size including LOG_OVERHEAD if buffer contains header up to\\n118:      *         magic byte, null otherwise\\n119:      * @throws CorruptRecordException if record size or magic is invalid\\n120:      */\\n121:     public Integer firstBatchSize() {\\n122:         if (buffer.remaining() < HEADER_SIZE_UP_TO_MAGIC)\\n123:             return null;\\n124:         return new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer, Integer.MAX_VALUE).nextBatchSize();\\n125:     }\\n126: \\n127:     /**\\n128:      * Filter the records into the provided ByteBuffer.\\n129:      *\\n130:      * @param filter                      The filter function\\n131:      * @param destinationBuffer           The byte buffer to write the filtered records to\\n132:      * @param decompressionBufferSupplier The supplier of ByteBuffer(s) used for decompression if supported. For small\\n133:      *                                    record batches, allocating a potentially large buffer (64 KB for LZ4) will\\n134:      *                                    dominate the cost of decompressing and iterating over the records in the\\n135:      *                                    batch. As such, a supplier that reuses buffers will have a significant\\n136:      *                                    performance impact.\\n137:      * @return A FilterResult with a summary of the output (for metrics) and potentially an overflow buffer\\n138:      */\\n139:     public FilterResult filterTo(RecordFilter filter, ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier) {\\n140:         return filterTo(batches(), filter, destinationBuffer, decompressionBufferSupplier);\\n141:     }\\n142: \\n143:     /**\\n144:      * Note: This method is also used to convert the first timestamp of the batch (which is usually the timestamp of the first record)\\n145:      * to the delete horizon of the tombstones or txn markers which are present in the batch.\\n146:      */\\n147:     private static FilterResult filterTo(Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches, RecordFilter filter,\\n148:                                          ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier) {\\n149:         FilterResult filterResult = new FilterResult(destinationBuffer);\\n150:         ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream = new ByteBufferOutputStream(destinationBuffer);\\n151:         for (MutableRecordBatch batch : batches) {\\n152:             final BatchRetentionResult batchRetentionResult = filter.checkBatchRetention(batch);\\n153:             final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = batchRetentionResult.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\\n154:             final BatchRetention batchRetention = batchRetentionResult.batchRetention;\\n155: \\n156:             filterResult.bytesRead += batch.sizeInBytes();\\n157: \\n158:             if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.DELETE)\\n159:                 continue;\\n160: \\n161:             final BatchFilterResult iterationResult = filterBatch(batch, decompressionBufferSupplier, filterResult,\\n162:                 filter);\\n163:             List<Record> retainedRecords = iterationResult.retainedRecords;\\n164:             boolean containsTombstones = iterationResult.containsTombstones;\\n165:             boolean writeOriginalBatch = iterationResult.writeOriginalBatch;\\n166:             long maxOffset = iterationResult.maxOffset;\\n167: \\n168:             if (!retainedRecords.isEmpty()) {\\n169:                 // we check if the delete horizon should be set to a new value\\n170:                 // in which case, we need to reset the base timestamp and overwrite the timestamp deltas\\n171:                 // if the batch does not contain tombstones, then we don't need to overwrite batch\\n172:                 boolean needToSetDeleteHorizon = (containsTombstones || containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) &&\\n173:                     batch.deleteHorizonMs().isEmpty();\\n174:                 if (writeOriginalBatch && !needToSetDeleteHorizon) {\\n175:                     batch.writeTo(bufferOutputStream);\\n176:                     filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, retainedRecords.size(), false);\\n177:                 } else {\\n178:                     long deleteHorizonMs;\\n179:                     if (needToSetDeleteHorizon)\\n180:                         deleteHorizonMs = filter.currentTime + filter.deleteRetentionMs;\\n181:                     else\\n182:                         deleteHorizonMs = batch.deleteHorizonMs().orElse(RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP);\\n183:                     try (final MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = buildRetainedRecordsInto(batch, retainedRecords,\\n184:                             bufferOutputStream, deleteHorizonMs)) {\\n185:                         MemoryRecords records = builder.build();\\n186:                         int filteredBatchSize = records.sizeInBytes();\\n187:                         MemoryRecordsBuilder.RecordsInfo info = builder.info();\\n188:                         filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(info.maxTimestamp, info.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp,\\n189:                             maxOffset, retainedRecords.size(), filteredBatchSize);\\n190:                     }\\n191:                 }\\n192:             } else if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.RETAIN_EMPTY) {\\n193:                 if (batch.magic() < RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2) // should never happen\\n194:                     throw new IllegalStateException(\\\"Empty batches are only supported for magic v2 and above\\\");\\n195: \\n196:                 bufferOutputStream.ensureRemaining(DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD);\\n197:                 DefaultRecordBatch.writeEmptyHeader(bufferOutputStream.buffer(), RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, batch.producerId(),\\n198:                         batch.producerEpoch(), batch.baseSequence(), batch.baseOffset(), batch.lastOffset(),\\n199:                         batch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), batch.timestampType(), batch.maxTimestamp(),\\n200:                         batch.isTransactional(), batch.isControlBatch());\\n201:                 filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, 0, true);\\n202:             }\\n203: \\n204:             // If we had to allocate a new buffer to fit the filtered buffer (see KAFKA-5316), return early to\\n205:             // avoid the need for additional allocations.\\n206:             ByteBuffer outputBuffer = bufferOutputStream.buffer();\\n207:             if (outputBuffer != destinationBuffer) {\\n208:                 filterResult.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\\n209:                 return filterResult;\\n210:             }\\n211:         }\\n212: \\n213:         return filterResult;\\n214:     }\\n215: \\n216:     private static BatchFilterResult filterBatch(RecordBatch batch,\\n217:                                                  BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier,\\n218:                                                  FilterResult filterResult,\\n219:                                                  RecordFilter filter) {\\n220:         try (final CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = batch.streamingIterator(decompressionBufferSupplier)) {\\n221:             long maxOffset = -1;\\n222:             boolean containsTombstones = false;\\n223:             // Convert records with old record versions\\n224:             boolean writeOriginalBatch = batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE;\\n225:             List<Record> retainedRecords = new ArrayList<>();\\n226:             while (iterator.hasNext()) {\\n227:                 Record record = iterator.next();\\n228:                 filterResult.messagesRead += 1;\\n229: \\n230:                 if (filter.shouldRetainRecord(batch, record)) {\\n231:                     if (record.offset() > maxOffset)\\n232:                         maxOffset = record.offset();\\n233: \\n234:                     retainedRecords.add(record);\\n235: \\n236:                     if (!record.hasValue()) {\\n237:                         containsTombstones = true;\\n238:                     }\\n239:                 } else {\\n240:                     writeOriginalBatch = false;\\n241:                 }\\n242:             }\\n243:             return new BatchFilterResult(retainedRecords, writeOriginalBatch, containsTombstones, maxOffset);\\n244:         }\\n245:     }\\n246: \\n247:     private static class BatchFilterResult {\\n248:         private final List<Record> retainedRecords;\\n249:         private final boolean writeOriginalBatch;\\n250:         private final boolean containsTombstones;\\n251:         private final long maxOffset;\\n252:         private BatchFilterResult(List<Record> retainedRecords,\\n253:                                   final boolean writeOriginalBatch,\\n254:                                   final boolean containsTombstones,\\n255:                                   final long maxOffset) {\\n256:             this.retainedRecords = retainedRecords;\\n257:             this.writeOriginalBatch = writeOriginalBatch;\\n258:             this.containsTombstones = containsTombstones;\\n259:             this.maxOffset = maxOffset;\\n260:         }\\n261:     }\\n262: \\n263:     private static MemoryRecordsBuilder buildRetainedRecordsInto(RecordBatch originalBatch,\\n264:                                                                  List<Record> retainedRecords,\\n265:                                                                  ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream,\\n266:                                                                  final long deleteHorizonMs) {\\n267:         Compression compression = Compression.of(originalBatch.compressionType()).build();\\n268:         // V0 has no timestamp type or timestamp, so we set the timestamp to CREATE_TIME and timestamp to NO_TIMESTAMP.\\n269:         // Note that this differs from produce up-conversion where the timestamp type topic config is used and the log append\\n270:         // time is generated if the config is LOG_APPEND_TIME. The reason for the different behavior is that there is\\n271:         // no appropriate log append time we can generate at compaction time.\\n272:         TimestampType timestampType = originalBatch.timestampType() == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE ?\\n273:                 TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : originalBatch.timestampType();\\n274:         long logAppendTime = timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME ?\\n275:                 originalBatch.maxTimestamp() : RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\\n276:         long baseOffset = originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 ?\\n277:                 originalBatch.baseOffset() : retainedRecords.get(0).offset();\\n278: \\n279:         // Convert records with older record versions to the current one\\n280:         MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferOutputStream, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE,\\n281:                 compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime, originalBatch.producerId(),\\n282:                 originalBatch.producerEpoch(), originalBatch.baseSequence(), originalBatch.isTransactional(),\\n283:                 originalBatch.isControlBatch(), originalBatch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), bufferOutputStream.limit(), deleteHorizonMs);\\n284: \\n285:         for (Record record : retainedRecords)\\n286:             builder.append(record);\\n287: \\n288:         if (originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2)\\n289:             // we must preserve the last offset from the initial batch in order to ensure that the\\n290:             // last sequence number from the batch remains even after compaction. Otherwise, the producer\\n291:             // could incorrectly see an out of sequence error.\\n292:             builder.overrideLastOffset(originalBatch.lastOffset());\\n293: \\n294:         return builder;\\n295:     }\\n296: \\n297:     /**\\n298:      * Get the byte buffer that backs this instance for reading.\\n299:      */\\n300:     public ByteBuffer buffer() {\\n301:         return buffer.duplicate();\\n302:     }\\n303: \\n304:     @Override\\n305:     public MemoryRecords slice(int position, int size) {\\n306:         if (position < 0)\\n307:             throw new IllegalArgumentException(\\\"Invalid position: \\\" + position + \\\" in read from \\\" + this);\\n308:         if (position > buffer.limit())\\n309:             throw new IllegalArgumentException(\\\"Slice from position \\\" + position + \\\" exceeds end position of \\\" + this);\\n310:         if (size < 0)\\n311:             throw new IllegalArgumentException(\\\"Invalid size: \\\" + size + \\\" in read from \\\" + this);\\n312: \\n313:         int availableBytes = Math.min(size, buffer.limit() - position);\\n314:         // As of now, clients module support Java11 hence can't use ByteBuffer::slice(position, size) method.\\n315:         // So we need to create a duplicate buffer and set the position and limit. Duplicate buffer\\n316:         // is backed by original bytes hence not the content but only the relative position and limit\\n317:         // are changed in the duplicate buffer. Once the position and limit are set, we can call the\\n318:         // slice method to get the sliced buffer, which is a backed by the original buffer with the\\n319:         // position reset to 0 and limit set to the size of the slice.\\n320:         ByteBuffer slicedBuffer = buffer.duplicate();\\n321:         slicedBuffer.position(position);\\n322:         slicedBuffer.limit(position + availableBytes);\\n323:         // Reset the position to 0 so that the sliced view has a relative position.\\n324:         slicedBuffer = slicedBuffer.slice();\\n325: \\n326:         return readableRecords(slicedBuffer);\\n327:     }\\n328: \\n329:     @Override\\n330:     public Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches() {\\n331:         return batches;\\n332:     }\\n333: \\n334:     @Override\\n335:     public String toString() {\\n336:         return \\\"MemoryRecords(size=\\\" + sizeInBytes() +\\n337:                 \\\", buffer=\\\" + buffer +\\n338:                 \\\")\\\";\\n339:     }\\n340: \\n341:     @Override\\n342:     public boolean equals(Object o) {\\n343:         if (this == o)\\n344:             return true;\\n345:         if (o == null || }\\n352: \\n353:     @Override\\n354:     public int hashCode() {\\n355:         return buffer.hashCode();\\n356:     }\\n357: \\n358:     public abstract static class RecordFilter {\\n359: The schema is given below:\\n47:  *\\n48:  * RecordBatch =>\\n49:  *  BaseOffset => Int64\\n50:  *  Length => Int32\\n51:  *  PartitionLeaderEpoch => Int32\\n52:  *  Magic => Int8\\n53:  *  CRC => Uint32\\n54:  *  Attributes => Int16\\n55:  *  LastOffsetDelta => Int32 // also serves as LastSequenceDelta\\n56:  *  BaseTimestamp => Int64\\n57:  *  MaxTimestamp => Int64\\n58:  *  ProducerId => Int64\\n59:  *  ProducerEpoch => Int16\\n60:  *  BaseSequence => Int32\\n61:  *  RecordsCount => Int32\\n62:  *  Records => [Record]\\n63:  *\\n64:  * Note that when compression is enabled (see attributes below), the compressed record data is serialized\\n65:  * directly following the count of the number of records.\\n66:  *\\n67:  * The CRC covers the data from the attributes to the end of the batch (i.e. all the bytes that follow the CRC). It is\\n68:  * located after the magic byte, which means that clients must parse the magic byte before deciding how to interpret\\n69:  * the bytes between the batch length and the magic byte. The partition leader epoch field is not included in the CRC\\n70:  * computation to avoid the need to recompute the CRC when this field is assigned for every batch that is received by\\n71:  * the broker. The CRC-32C (Castagnoli) polynomial is used for the computation.\\n72:  *\\n73:  * On Compaction: Unlike the older message formats, magic v2 and above preserves the first and last offset/sequence\\n74:  * numbers from the original batch when the log is cleaned. This is required in order to be able to restore the\\n75:  * producer's state when the log is reloaded. If we did not retain the last sequence number, then following\\n76:  * a partition leader failure, once the new leader has rebuilt the producer state from the log, the next sequence\\n77:  * expected number would no longer be in sync with what was written by the client. This would cause an\\n78:  * unexpected OutOfOrderSequence error, which is typically fatal. The base sequence number must be preserved for\\n79:  * duplicate checking: the broker checks incoming Produce requests for duplicates by verifying that the first and\\n80:  * last sequence numbers of the incoming batch match the last from that producer.\\n81:  *\\n82:  * Note that if all of the records in a batch are removed during compaction, the broker may still retain an empty\\n83:  * batch header in order to preserve the producer sequence information as described above. These empty batches\\n84:  * are retained only until either a new sequence number is written by the corresponding producer or the producerId\\n85:  * is expired from lack of activity.\\n86:  *\\n87:  * There is no similar need to preserve the timestamp from the original batch after compaction. The BaseTimestamp\\n88:  * field therefore reflects the timestamp of the first record in the batch in most cases. If the batch is empty, the\\n89:  * BaseTimestamp will be set to -1 (NO_TIMESTAMP). If the delete horizon flag is set to 1, the BaseTimestamp\\n90:  * will be set to the time at which tombstone records and aborted transaction markers in the batch should be removed.\\n91:  *\\n92:  * Similarly, the MaxTimestamp field reflects the maximum timestamp of the current records if the timestamp type\\n93:  * is CREATE_TIME. For LOG_APPEND_TIME, on the other hand, the MaxTimestamp field reflects the timestamp set\\n94:  * by the broker and is preserved after compaction. Additionally, the MaxTimestamp of an empty batch always retains\\n95:  * the previous value prior to becoming empty.\\n96:  *\\n97:  * The current attributes are given below:\\n98:  *\\n99:  *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n100:  *  | Unused (7-15) | Delete Horizon Flag (6) | Control (5) | Transactional (4) | Timestamp Type (3) | Compression Type (0-2) |\\n101:  *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n102:  */\\n103: public class DefaultRecordBatch extends   "command": "create",
  "file_text": "/*\n * Licensed to the Apache Software Foundation (ASF) under one or more\n * contributor license agreements. See the NOTICE file distributed with\n * this work for additional information regarding copyright ownership.\n * The ASF licenses this file to You under the Apache License, Version 2.0\n * (the \"License\"); you may not use this file except in compliance with\n * the License. You may obtain a copy of the License at\n *\n *    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n *\n * Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n * distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n * WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n * See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n * limitations under the License.\n */\npackage org.apache.kafka.common.record.internal;\n\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.InvalidRecordException;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.KafkaException;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.compress.Compression;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.errors.CorruptRecordException;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.header.Header;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.record.TimestampType;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.utils.BufferSupplier;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.utils.ByteBufferOutputStream;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.utils.ByteUtils;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.utils.CloseableIterator;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.utils.Crc32C;\n\nimport java.io.IOException;\nimport java.io.InputStream;\nimport java.nio.BufferUnderflowException;\nimport java.nio.ByteBuffer;\nimport java.util.ArrayList;\nimport java.util.Collections;\nimport java.util.Iterator;\nimport java.util.List;\nimport java.util.NoSuchElementException;\nimport java.util.Objects;\nimport java.util.OptionalLong;\n\nimport static org.apache.kafka.common.record.internal.Records.LOG_OVERHEAD;\n\n/**\n * {@link RecordBatch} implementation for magic v2 and above. This class provides a zero-copy,\n * {@link ByteBuffer}-backed view of a single record batch as it appears on the wire or in the\n * Kafka log. All header fields are read directly from the underlying buffer without copying,\n * making header access O(1) and allocation-free.\n *\n * <h2>Wire format</h2>\n * <pre>\n * RecordBatch =&gt;\n *   BaseOffset            =&gt; Int64\n *   Length                =&gt; Int32\n *   PartitionLeaderEpoch  =&gt; Int32\n *   Magic                 =&gt; Int8\n *   CRC                   =&gt; Uint32\n *   Attributes            =&gt; Int16\n *   LastOffsetDelta       =&gt; Int32   // also serves as LastSequenceDelta\n *   BaseTimestamp         =&gt; Int64\n *   MaxTimestamp          =&gt; Int64\n *   ProducerId            =&gt; Int64\n *   ProducerEpoch         =&gt; Int16\n *   BaseSequence          =&gt; Int32\n *   RecordsCount          =&gt; Int32\n *   Records               =&gt; [Record]\n * </pre>\n *\n * <p>When compression is enabled (see the {@code Attributes} field), the compressed record data\n * is serialised directly after the record count field. The CRC covers all bytes from\n * {@code Attributes} to the end of the batch and uses the CRC-32C (Castagnoli) polynomial.\n * The {@code PartitionLeaderEpoch} field is intentionally excluded from the CRC so that brokers\n * can assign it without recomputing the checksum.\n *\n * <h2>Attribute bit layout</h2>\n * <pre>\n * Bits 15\u20137 : Unused\n * Bit  6    : Delete Horizon Flag\n * Bit  5    : Control\n * Bit  4    : Transactional\n * Bit  3    : Timestamp Type (0 = CREATE_TIME, 1 = LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n * Bits 2\u20130  : Compression Type\n * </pre>\n *\n * <h2>Compaction behaviour</h2>\n * <p>Unlike the legacy message formats, magic v2 preserves the original\n * {@link #baseOffset()}/{@link #baseSequence()} and {@link #lastOffset()}/{@link #lastSequence()}\n * values after log compaction. This is required so that the broker can reconstruct producer\n * state after a leader failover and correctly detect duplicate produce requests. If all records\n * in a batch are removed during compaction, the broker may retain an empty batch header (with\n * {@link #RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD} bytes) until the producer writes a new sequence number or the\n * producer id expires.\n *\n * <h2>Timestamp semantics after compaction</h2>\n * <p>The {@code BaseTimestamp} field normally holds the timestamp of the first record. When the\n * delete-horizon flag is set, it instead holds the time at which tombstone records and aborted\n * transaction markers in the batch should be deleted. The {@code MaxTimestamp} field reflects\n * the maximum record timestamp for {@link TimestampType#CREATE_TIME} batches, or the\n * broker-assigned log-append time for {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME} batches; the latter\n * is preserved across compaction.\n *\n * <h2>Performance characteristics</h2>\n * <ul>\n *   <li>Header field reads are O(1) and involve no heap allocation.</li>\n *   <li>Iterating over uncompressed records ({@link #iterator()}, {@link #streamingIterator})\n *       reads directly from the backing buffer without copying.</li>\n *   <li>Iterating over compressed records requires decompression. Use\n *       {@link #streamingIterator(BufferSupplier)} with a pooling {@link BufferSupplier} to\n *       amortise the cost of allocating the decompression buffer across many batches.</li>\n *   <li>{@link #iterator()} on a compressed batch eagerly decompresses all records into a\n *       heap-allocated list so that the underlying stream can be closed immediately. Prefer\n *       {@link #streamingIterator(BufferSupplier)} when memory efficiency is important.</li>\n * </ul>\n *\n * <p><b>Thread safety:</b> Instances of this class are <em>not</em> thread-safe. The mutable\n * operations exposed by {@link MutableRecordBatch} ({@link #setLastOffset},\n * {@link #setMaxTimestamp}, {@link #setPartitionLeaderEpoch}) modify the backing\n * {@link ByteBuffer} in place and must not be called concurrently with any other operation on\n * the same instance.\n *\n * @see RecordBatch\n * @see MutableRecordBatch\n * @see MemoryRecords\n * @see MemoryRecordsBuilder\n */\npublic class DefaultRecordBatch extends AbstractRecordBatch implements MutableRecordBatch {\n    static final int BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET = 0;\n    static final int BASE_OFFSET_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int LENGTH_OFFSET = BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET + BASE_OFFSET_LENGTH;\n    static final int LENGTH_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET = LENGTH_OFFSET + LENGTH_LENGTH;\n    static final int PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int MAGIC_OFFSET = PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET + PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_LENGTH;\n    static final int MAGIC_LENGTH = 1;\n    public static final int CRC_OFFSET = MAGIC_OFFSET + MAGIC_LENGTH;\n    static final int CRC_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET = CRC_OFFSET + CRC_LENGTH;\n    static final int ATTRIBUTE_LENGTH = 2;\n    public static final int LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET = ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET + ATTRIBUTE_LENGTH;\n    static final int LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET = LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET + LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_LENGTH;\n    static final int BASE_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET = BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET + BASE_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH;\n    static final int MAX_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET = MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET + MAX_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH;\n    static final int PRODUCER_ID_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET = PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET + PRODUCER_ID_LENGTH;\n    static final int PRODUCER_EPOCH_LENGTH = 2;\n    static final int BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET = PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET + PRODUCER_EPOCH_LENGTH;\n    static final int BASE_SEQUENCE_LENGTH = 4;\n    public static final int RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET = BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET + BASE_SEQUENCE_LENGTH;\n    static final int RECORDS_COUNT_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int RECORDS_OFFSET = RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET + RECORDS_COUNT_LENGTH;\n    public static final int RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD = RECORDS_OFFSET;\n\n    private static final byte COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK = 0x07;\n    private static final byte TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK = 0x10;\n    private static final int CONTROL_FLAG_MASK = 0x20;\n    private static final byte DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK = 0x40;\n    private static final byte TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK = 0x08;\n\n    private final ByteBuffer buffer;\n\n    DefaultRecordBatch(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        this.buffer = buffer;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public byte magic() {\n        return buffer.get(MAGIC_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void ensureValid() {\n        if (sizeInBytes() < RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD)\n            throw new CorruptRecordException(\"Record batch is corrupt (the size \" + sizeInBytes() +\n                    \" is smaller than the minimum allowed overhead \" + RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD + \")\");\n\n        if (!isValid())\n            throw new CorruptRecordException(\"Record is corrupt (stored crc = \" + checksum()\n                    + \", computed crc = \" + computeChecksum() + \")\");\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Gets the base timestamp of the batch, which is used to reconstruct individual record\n     * timestamps from their stored delta values.\n     *\n     * <p>When the delete-horizon flag is set in the batch attributes, this field holds the\n     * delete horizon timestamp instead of the first-record timestamp. Callers that need to\n     * distinguish between the two cases should check {@link #deleteHorizonMs()} first.\n     *\n     * @return The base timestamp in milliseconds since the Unix epoch, or\n     *         {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP} ({@code -1}) for empty batches\n     */\n    public long baseTimestamp() {\n        return buffer.getLong(BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long maxTimestamp() {\n        return buffer.getLong(MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TimestampType timestampType() {\n        return (attributes() & TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK) == 0 ? TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long baseOffset() {\n        return buffer.getLong(BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long lastOffset() {\n        return baseOffset() + lastOffsetDelta();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long producerId() {\n        return buffer.getLong(PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public short producerEpoch() {\n        return buffer.getShort(PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int baseSequence() {\n        return buffer.getInt(BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private int lastOffsetDelta() {\n        return buffer.getInt(LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int lastSequence() {\n        int baseSequence = baseSequence();\n        if (baseSequence == RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE)\n            return RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE;\n        return incrementSequence(baseSequence, lastOffsetDelta());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public CompressionType compressionType() {\n        return CompressionType.forId(attributes() & COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int sizeInBytes() {\n        return LOG_OVERHEAD + buffer.getInt(LENGTH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private int count() {\n        return buffer.getInt(RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Integer countOrNull() {\n        return count();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Serialize this batch into a {@link ByteBuffer} by copying the backing buffer.\n     *\n     * <p>The destination buffer's position is advanced by {@link #sizeInBytes()} bytes.\n     * This is a bulk memory copy and does not involve re-encoding or re-compression.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The destination buffer; must have at least {@link #sizeInBytes()} bytes\n     *               of remaining capacity\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void writeTo(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        buffer.put(this.buffer.duplicate());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Serialize this batch into a {@link ByteBufferOutputStream} by copying the backing buffer.\n     *\n     * <p>This is a bulk memory copy and does not involve re-encoding or re-compression.\n     *\n     * @param outputStream The destination stream; must have sufficient remaining capacity\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void writeTo(ByteBufferOutputStream outputStream) {\n        outputStream.write(this.buffer.duplicate());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isTransactional() {\n        return (attributes() & TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    private boolean hasDeleteHorizonMs() {\n        return (attributes() & DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public OptionalLong deleteHorizonMs() {\n        if (hasDeleteHorizonMs())\n            return OptionalLong.of(buffer.getLong(BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET));\n        else\n            return OptionalLong.empty();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isControlBatch() {\n        return (attributes() & CONTROL_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int partitionLeaderEpoch() {\n        return buffer.getInt(PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Open an {@link InputStream} over the (possibly compressed) record data section of this\n     * batch, positioned immediately after the batch header.\n     *\n     * <p>If the batch is compressed, the returned stream transparently decompresses the data\n     * using the codec indicated by {@link #compressionType()}. The caller is responsible for\n     * closing the stream when done to release any decompression resources.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance note:</b> Decompression buffers are obtained from the supplied\n     * {@link BufferSupplier}. Using a pooling supplier avoids repeated large allocations\n     * (e.g., 64 KB for LZ4) when processing many small batches.\n     *\n     * @param bufferSupplier Supplier of {@link ByteBuffer}s used as decompression scratch space;\n     *                       must not be {@code null}\n     * @return An {@link InputStream} positioned at the first record byte; the caller must close it\n     */\n    public InputStream recordInputStream(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        final ByteBuffer buffer = this.buffer.duplicate();\n        buffer.position(RECORDS_OFFSET);\n        return Compression.of(compressionType()).build().wrapForInput(buffer, magic(), bufferSupplier);\n    }\n\n    private CloseableIterator<Record> compressedIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier, boolean skipKeyValue) {\n        final InputStream inputStream = recordInputStream(bufferSupplier);\n\n        if (skipKeyValue) {\n            return new StreamRecordIterator(inputStream) {\n                @Override\n                protected Record doReadRecord(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) throws IOException {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readPartiallyFrom(inputStream, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                }\n            };\n        } else {\n            return new StreamRecordIterator(inputStream) {\n                @Override\n                protected Record doReadRecord(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) throws IOException {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readFrom(inputStream, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                }\n            };\n        }\n    }\n\n    private CloseableIterator<Record> uncompressedIterator() {\n        final ByteBuffer buffer = this.buffer.duplicate();\n        buffer.position(RECORDS_OFFSET);\n        return new RecordIterator() {\n            @Override\n            protected Record readNext(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) {\n                try {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readFrom(buffer, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                } catch (BufferUnderflowException e) {\n                    throw new InvalidRecordException(\"Incorrect declared batch size, premature EOF reached\");\n                }\n            }\n            @Override\n            protected boolean ensureNoneRemaining() {\n                return !buffer.hasRemaining();\n            }\n            @Override\n            public void close() {}\n        };\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return an iterator over all {@link Record}s in this batch.\n     *\n     * <p>For uncompressed batches, records are read directly from the backing buffer with no\n     * heap allocation beyond the {@link Record} wrappers themselves.\n     *\n     * <p>For compressed batches, this method eagerly decompresses the entire record set into a\n     * heap-allocated {@link List} so that the underlying decompression stream can be closed\n     * immediately. This avoids resource leaks but increases peak memory usage proportionally to\n     * the uncompressed batch size. Callers that require lower memory overhead should use\n     * {@link #streamingIterator(BufferSupplier)} instead.\n     *\n     * @return An iterator over the decoded records; never {@code null}\n     * @throws InvalidRecordException if the declared record count does not match the actual\n     *         number of records found in the batch\n     */\n    @Override\n    public Iterator<Record> iterator() {\n        if (count() == 0)\n            return Collections.emptyIterator();\n\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // for a normal iterator, we cannot ensure that the underlying compression stream is closed,\n        // so we decompress the full record set here. Use cases which call for a lower memory footprint\n        // can use `streamingIterator` at the cost of additional complexity\n        try (CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = compressedIterator(BufferSupplier.NO_CACHING, false)) {\n            List<Record> records = new ArrayList<>(count());\n            while (iterator.hasNext())\n                records.add(iterator.next());\n            return records.iterator();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return a {@link CloseableIterator} that skips deserialisation of record keys, values, and\n     * headers, yielding lightweight {@link Record} stubs that carry only offset and timestamp\n     * metadata.\n     *\n     * <p>For uncompressed batches, skipping key/value is not beneficial because the underlying\n     * {@link ByteBuffer#position(int)} skip is no faster than a full read; the full uncompressed\n     * iterator is returned in that case.\n     *\n     * <p>For compressed batches, this iterator decompresses lazily (streaming), which avoids\n     * materialising the full record set. The caller must close the iterator to release the\n     * decompression stream.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance note:</b> This iterator is intended for use cases such as log validation\n     * where key/value content is not needed, reducing both CPU (no key/value parsing) and heap\n     * allocation overhead.\n     *\n     * @param bufferSupplier Supplier of {@link ByteBuffer}s used as decompression scratch space\n     *                       for compressed batches; must not be {@code null}\n     * @return A {@link CloseableIterator} over partial records; callers must close it\n     */\n    @Override\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> skipKeyValueIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (count() == 0) {\n            return CloseableIterator.wrap(Collections.emptyIterator());\n        }\n\n        /*\n         * For uncompressed iterator, it is actually not worth skipping key / value / headers at all since\n         * its ByteBufferInputStream's skip() function is less efficient compared with just reading it actually\n         * as it will allocate new byte array.\n         */\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // we define this to be a closable iterator so that caller (i.e. the log validator) needs to close it\n        // while we can save memory footprint of not decompressing the full record set ahead of time\n        return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, true);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return a lazy, streaming {@link CloseableIterator} over the records in this batch.\n     *\n     * <p>For compressed batches, decompression is performed on demand as each record is\n     * requested via {@link Iterator#next()}, rather than up front. This reduces peak memory\n     * usage compared to {@link #iterator()} at the cost of keeping the decompression stream\n     * open until the iterator is closed. Callers <em>must</em> close the returned iterator.\n     *\n     * <p>For uncompressed batches, the iterator reads directly from the backing buffer and\n     * {@link CloseableIterator#close()} is a no-op.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance note:</b> Reusing decompression buffers via a pooling\n     * {@link BufferSupplier} can significantly reduce allocation pressure when processing many\n     * small batches.\n     *\n     * @param bufferSupplier Supplier of {@link ByteBuffer}s used as decompression scratch space;\n     *                       must not be {@code null}\n     * @return A {@link CloseableIterator} over the decoded records; callers must close it\n     */\n    @Override\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> streamingIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (isCompressed())\n            return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, false);\n        else\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Update the base offset of this batch in place so that the last offset equals the given\n     * value.\n     *\n     * <p>This method is used by the broker to assign log offsets to a batch received from a\n     * producer before appending it to the partition log. The base offset is computed as\n     * {@code offset - lastOffsetDelta} so that the last offset of the batch equals\n     * {@code offset}.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Note:</b> This operation modifies the backing {@link ByteBuffer} directly and does\n     * not recompute the CRC. The CRC is not invalidated because the base offset field is\n     * excluded from the CRC computation.\n     *\n     * @param offset The desired last offset for this batch; must be non-negative\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void setLastOffset(long offset) {\n        buffer.putLong(BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET, offset - lastOffsetDelta());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Update the max timestamp and timestamp type of this batch in place, recomputing the\n     * CRC-32C checksum if either value changes.\n     *\n     * <p>This method is used by the broker when assigning {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME}\n     * to a batch. When log-append time is used, the max timestamp field is overwritten with the\n     * broker's wall-clock time and the timestamp-type bit in the attributes field is updated\n     * accordingly. Individual record timestamp deltas are <em>not</em> rewritten (which would\n     * require recompression); instead, consumers ignore per-record timestamps when the batch\n     * timestamp type is {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME}.\n     *\n     * <p>If the supplied timestamp type and value are identical to the current values, this\n     * method is a no-op and the CRC is not recomputed.\n     *\n     * @param timestampType The new timestamp type; must not be\n     *                      {@link TimestampType#NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE}\n     * @param maxTimestamp  The new maximum timestamp in milliseconds since the Unix epoch\n     * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code timestampType} is\n     *                                  {@link TimestampType#NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE}\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void setMaxTimestamp(TimestampType timestampType, long maxTimestamp) {\n        long currentMaxTimestamp = maxTimestamp();\n        // We don't need to recompute crc if the timestamp is not updated.\n        if (timestampType() == timestampType && currentMaxTimestamp == maxTimestamp)\n            return;\n\n        byte attributes = computeAttributes(compressionType(), timestampType, isTransactional(), isControlBatch(), hasDeleteHorizonMs());\n        buffer.putShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, attributes);\n        buffer.putLong(MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, maxTimestamp);\n        long crc = computeChecksum();\n        ByteUtils.writeUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET, crc);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Update the partition leader epoch of this batch in place.\n     *\n     * <p>The partition leader epoch is assigned by the broker when the batch is appended to the\n     * log. Because this field is excluded from the CRC computation, updating it does not require\n     * a CRC recomputation.\n     *\n     * @param epoch The partition leader epoch to assign; must be non-negative\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void setPartitionLeaderEpoch(int epoch) {\n        buffer.putInt(PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET, epoch);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long checksum() {\n        return ByteUtils.readUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether the CRC-32C checksum stored in this batch matches the checksum computed\n     * over the batch header and records.\n     *\n     * <p>This method also verifies that the batch is at least {@link #RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD}\n     * bytes long, which is the minimum size for a valid (possibly empty) v2 batch.\n     *\n     * @return {@code true} if the batch is structurally valid and the checksum matches;\n     *         {@code false} otherwise\n     */\n    public boolean isValid() {\n        return sizeInBytes() >= RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD && checksum() == computeChecksum();\n    }\n\n    private long computeChecksum() {\n        return Crc32C.compute(buffer, ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, buffer.limit() - ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private byte attributes() {\n        // note we're not using the second byte of attributes\n        return (byte) buffer.getShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        DefaultRecordBatch that = (DefaultRecordBatch) o;\n        return Objects.equals(buffer, that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer != null ? buffer.hashCode() : 0;\n    }\n\n    private static byte computeAttributes(CompressionType type, TimestampType timestampType,\n                                          boolean isTransactional, boolean isControl, boolean isDeleteHorizonSet) {\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Timestamp type must be provided to compute attributes for message \" +\n                    \"format v2 and above\");\n\n        byte attributes = isTransactional ? TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK : 0;\n        if (isControl)\n            attributes |= CONTROL_FLAG_MASK;\n        if (type.id > 0)\n            attributes |= (byte) (COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK & type.id);\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            attributes |= TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK;\n        if (isDeleteHorizonSet)\n            attributes |= DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK;\n        return attributes;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write an empty (zero-record) batch header into the given buffer at its current position.\n     *\n     * <p>Empty batch headers are retained in the log after compaction to preserve producer\n     * sequence information. The batch will have a record count of zero and its size will be\n     * exactly {@link #RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD} bytes.\n     *\n     * @param buffer               The destination buffer; must have at least\n     *                             {@link #RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD} bytes of remaining capacity\n     * @param magic                The magic byte; must be {@link RecordBatch#MAGIC_VALUE_V2} or higher\n     * @param producerId           The producer id to embed in the header\n     * @param producerEpoch        The producer epoch to embed in the header\n     * @param baseSequence         The base sequence number to embed in the header\n     * @param baseOffset           The base offset of the original batch\n     * @param lastOffset           The last offset of the original batch\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch to embed in the header\n     * @param timestampType        The timestamp type; must not be\n     *                             {@link TimestampType#NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE}\n     * @param timestamp            The timestamp to use as the max timestamp of the empty batch\n     * @param isTransactional      {@code true} if the batch belongs to a transaction\n     * @param isControlRecord      {@code true} if the batch is a control batch\n     */\n    public static void writeEmptyHeader(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                        byte magic,\n                                        long producerId,\n                                        short producerEpoch,\n                                        int baseSequence,\n                                        long baseOffset,\n                                        long lastOffset,\n                                        int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                        TimestampType timestampType,\n                                        long timestamp,\n                                        boolean isTransactional,\n                                        boolean isControlRecord) {\n        int offsetDelta = (int) (lastOffset - baseOffset);\n        writeHeader(buffer, baseOffset, offsetDelta, DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD, magic,\n                    CompressionType.NONE, timestampType, RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP, timestamp, producerId,\n                    producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, isControlRecord, false, partitionLeaderEpoch, 0);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Encode a complete v2 batch header into the given buffer at its current position and\n     * compute and write the CRC-32C checksum.\n     *\n     * <p>After this method returns, the buffer's position is advanced to\n     * {@code position + RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD}. The caller is responsible for writing the\n     * encoded record data immediately after the header.\n     *\n     * @param buffer               The destination buffer; must have at least\n     *                             {@link #RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD} bytes of remaining capacity\n     * @param baseOffset           The base (first) offset of the batch\n     * @param lastOffsetDelta      The difference between the last and base offsets\n     * @param sizeInBytes          The total size of the batch in bytes, including the header\n     * @param magic                The magic byte; must be {@link RecordBatch#MAGIC_VALUE_V2} or higher\n     * @param compressionType      The compression codec used for the record data\n     * @param timestampType        The timestamp type; must not be\n     *                             {@link TimestampType#NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE}\n     * @param baseTimestamp        The timestamp of the first record, or\n     *                             {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP} for empty batches\n     * @param maxTimestamp         The maximum timestamp among all records in the batch\n     * @param producerId           The producer id\n     * @param epoch                The producer epoch\n     * @param sequence             The base sequence number\n     * @param isTransactional      {@code true} if the batch belongs to a transaction\n     * @param isControlBatch       {@code true} if the batch is a control batch\n     * @param isDeleteHorizonSet   {@code true} if the delete-horizon flag should be set in the\n     *                             attributes, causing {@code baseTimestamp} to be interpreted as\n     *                             the delete horizon rather than the first-record timestamp\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param numRecords           The number of records in the batch\n     * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code magic} is less than\n     *                                  {@link RecordBatch#CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE}, or if\n     *                                  {@code baseTimestamp} is negative and not equal to\n     *                                  {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP}\n     */\n    public static void writeHeader(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                   long baseOffset,\n                                   int lastOffsetDelta,\n                                   int sizeInBytes,\n                                   byte magic,\n                                   CompressionType compressionType,\n                                   TimestampType timestampType,\n                                   long baseTimestamp,\n                                   long maxTimestamp,\n                                   long producerId,\n                                   short epoch,\n                                   int sequence,\n                                   boolean isTransactional,\n                                   boolean isControlBatch,\n                                   boolean isDeleteHorizonSet,\n                                   int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                   int numRecords) {\n        if (magic < RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid magic value \" + magic);\n        if (baseTimestamp < 0 && baseTimestamp != NO_TIMESTAMP)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid message timestamp \" + baseTimestamp);\n\n        short attributes = computeAttributes(compressionType, timestampType, isTransactional, isControlBatch, isDeleteHorizonSet);\n\n        int position = buffer.position();\n        buffer.putLong(position + BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET, baseOffset);\n        buffer.putInt(position + LENGTH_OFFSET, sizeInBytes - LOG_OVERHEAD);\n        buffer.putInt(position + PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET, partitionLeaderEpoch);\n        buffer.put(position + MAGIC_OFFSET, magic);\n        buffer.putShort(position + ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, attributes);\n        buffer.putLong(position + BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, baseTimestamp);\n        buffer.putLong(position + MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, maxTimestamp);\n        buffer.putInt(position + LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET, lastOffsetDelta);\n        buffer.putLong(position + PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET, producerId);\n        buffer.putShort(position + PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET, epoch);\n        buffer.putInt(position + BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET, sequence);\n        buffer.putInt(position + RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET, numRecords);\n        long crc = Crc32C.compute(buffer, ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, sizeInBytes - ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n        buffer.putInt(position + CRC_OFFSET, (int) crc);\n        buffer.position(position + RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"RecordBatch(magic=\" + magic() + \", offsets=[\" + baseOffset() + \", \" + lastOffset() + \"], \" +\n                \"sequence=[\" + baseSequence() + \", \" + lastSequence() + \"], \" +\n                \"partitionLeaderEpoch=\" + partitionLeaderEpoch() + \", \" +\n                \"isTransactional=\" + isTransactional() + \", isControlBatch=\" + isControlBatch() + \", \" +\n                \"compression=\" + compressionType() + \", timestampType=\" + timestampType() + \", crc=\" + checksum() + \")\";\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Compute the serialised size in bytes of a v2 batch that would contain the given records,\n     * using the supplied base offset to calculate per-record offset deltas.\n     *\n     * <p>This method iterates over all records to accumulate their variable-length encoded sizes\n     * and is therefore O(n) in the number of records. The result does not account for\n     * compression; use it as an upper bound when compression is enabled.\n     *\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset of the batch, used to compute per-record offset deltas\n     * @param records    The records that would be included in the batch; must not be {@code null}\n     * @return The total size in bytes of the batch header plus all encoded records, or {@code 0}\n     *         if {@code records} is empty\n     */\n    public static int sizeInBytes(long baseOffset, Iterable<Record> records) {\n        Iterator<Record> iterator = records.iterator();\n        if (!iterator.hasNext())\n            return 0;\n\n        int size = RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD;\n        Long baseTimestamp = null;\n        while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n            Record record = iterator.next();\n            int offsetDelta = (int) (record.offset() - baseOffset);\n            if (baseTimestamp == null)\n                baseTimestamp = record.timestamp();\n            long timestampDelta = record.timestamp() - baseTimestamp;\n            size += DefaultRecord.sizeInBytes(offsetDelta, timestampDelta, record.key(), record.value(),\n                    record.headers());\n        }\n        return size;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Compute the serialised size in bytes of a v2 batch that would contain the given\n     * {@link SimpleRecord}s, assuming a base offset of zero.\n     *\n     * <p>This method iterates over all records to accumulate their variable-length encoded sizes\n     * and is therefore O(n) in the number of records. public static int decrementSequence(int sequence, int decrement) {\n        if (sequence < decrement)\n            return Integer.MAX_VALUE - (decrement - sequence) + 1;\n        return sequence - decrement;\n    }\n\n    // visible for testing\n    abstract class RecordIterator implements CloseableIterator<Record> {\n        private final Long logAppendTime;\n        private final long This is the primary representation used by Kafka\n * producers, consumers, and the broker's network layer when record data is held in heap memory.\n *\n * <h2>Role in the Kafka protocol</h2>\n * <p>{@code MemoryRecords} sits at the boundary between the network/storage layer and the\n * application layer. Producers build instances via {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} (or the\n * {@link #builder} factory methods) and send them to the broker. The broker receives them,\n * optionally mutates batch metadata in place (e.g., assigning log offsets and log-append\n * timestamps via {@link MutableRecordBatch}), and appends them to the partition log. Consumers\n * receive {@code MemoryRecords} instances from the broker and iterate over the contained\n * {@link RecordBatch}es and {@link Record}s.\n *\n * <h2>Construction</h2>\n * <p>There are two ways to obtain a {@code MemoryRecords} instance:\n * <ol>\n *   <li><b>Reading an existing buffer:</b> Use {@link #readableRecords(ByteBuffer)} to wrap a\n *       buffer that already contains encoded batch data. The buffer is not copied; the\n *       {@code MemoryRecords} instance holds a reference to it.</li>\n *   <li><b>Building a new batch:</b> Use one of the {@link #builder} factory methods to obtain\n *       a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder}, append records to it, and call\n *       {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder#build()} to produce the final {@code MemoryRecords}. The\n *       convenience {@code withRecords}, {@code withIdempotentRecords},\n *       {@code withTransactionalRecords}, and {@code withEndTransactionMarker} methods combine\n *       these steps into a single call.</li>\n * </ol>\n *\n * <h2>Performance characteristics</h2>\n * <ul>\n *   <li>Batch iteration ({@link #batches()}, {@link #batchIterator()}) is zero-copy: each\n *       {@link MutableRecordBatch} is a lightweight view over a slice of the backing buffer.</li>\n *   <li>Record iteration ({@link Records#records()}) may require decompression. Use\n *       {@link RecordBatch#streamingIterator(BufferSupplier)} with a pooling\n *       {@link BufferSupplier} to amortise decompression buffer allocation costs.</li>\n *   <li>{@link #validBytes()} is computed lazily on first call and then cached; subsequent\n *       calls are O(1).</li>\n *   <li>{@link #filterTo(RecordFilter, ByteBuffer, BufferSupplier)} performs record-level\n *       filtering in a single pass and writes the retained records directly into the supplied\n *       destination buffer, avoiding an extra copy.</li>\n *   <li>{@link #slice(int, int)} returns a zero-copy view backed by the same underlying bytes.</li>\n * </ul>\n *\n * <p><b>Thread safety:</b> Instances of this class are <em>not</em> thread-safe. The backing\n * {@link ByteBuffer} is shared by reference, and concurrent reads or writes (including the\n * in-place mutations performed by {@link MutableRecordBatch} methods) require external\n * synchronisation.\n *\n * @see RecordBatch\n * @see DefaultRecordBatch\n * @see MemoryRecordsBuilder\n * @see Records\n */\npublic class MemoryRecords extends AbstractRecords {\n    /** A singleton empty {@code MemoryRecords} instance backed by a zero-capacity buffer. */\n    public static final MemoryRecords EMPTY = MemoryRecords.readableRecords(ByteBuffer.allocate(0));\n\n    private final ByteBuffer buffer;\n\n    private final Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches = this::batchIterator;\n\n    private int validBytes = -1;\n\n    // Construct a writable memory records\n    private MemoryRecords(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        Objects.requireNonNull(buffer, \"buffer should not be null\");\n        this.buffer = buffer;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return the total number of bytes in the backing buffer, including any partial or trailing\n     * batches that may not be parseable.\n     *\n     * <p>This value equals the limit of the underlying {@link ByteBuffer} and is O(1).
