static BatchFilterResult filterBatch(RecordBatch batch,\n                                                 BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier,\n                                                 FilterResult filterResult,\n                                                 RecordFilter filter) {\n        try (final CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = batch.streamingIterator(decompressionBufferSupplier)) {\n            long maxOffset = -1;\n            boolean containsTombstones = false;\n            // Convert records with old record versions\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE;\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = new ArrayList<>();\n            while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n                Record record = iterator.next();\n                filterResult.messagesRead += 1;\n\n                if (filter.shouldRetainRecord(batch, record)) {\n                    if (record.offset() > maxOffset)\n                        maxOffset = record.offset();\n\n                    retainedRecords.add(record);\n\n                    if (!record.hasValue()) {\n                        containsTombstones = true;\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    writeOriginalBatch = false;\n                }\n            }\n            return new BatchFilterResult(retainedRecords, writeOriginalBatch, containsTombstones, maxOffset);\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static class BatchFilterResult {\n        private final List<Record> retainedRecords;\n        private final boolean writeOriginalBatch;\n        private final boolean containsTombstones;\n        private final long maxOffset;\n        private BatchFilterResult(List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                  final boolean writeOriginalBatch,\n                                  final boolean containsTombstones,\n                                  final long maxOffset) {\n            this.retainedRecords = retainedRecords;\n            this.writeOriginalBatch = writeOriginalBatch;\n            this.containsTombstones = containsTombstones;\n            this.maxOffset = maxOffset;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static MemoryRecordsBuilder buildRetainedRecordsInto(RecordBatch originalBatch,\n                                                                 List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                                                 ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream,\n                                                                 final long deleteHorizonMs) {\n        Compression compression = Compression.of(originalBatch.compressionType()).build();\n        // V0 has no timestamp type or timestamp, so we set the timestamp to CREATE_TIME and timestamp to NO_TIMESTAMP.\n        // Note that this differs from produce up-conversion where the timestamp type topic config is used and the log append\n        // time is generated if the config is LOG_APPEND_TIME. The reason for the different behavior is that there is\n        // no appropriate log append time we can generate at compaction time.\n        TimestampType timestampType = originalBatch.timestampType() == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE ?\n                TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : originalBatch.timestampType();\n        long logAppendTime = timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME ?\n                originalBatch.maxTimestamp() : RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        long baseOffset = originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 ?\n                originalBatch.baseOffset() : retainedRecords.get(0).offset();\n\n        // Convert records with older record versions to the current one\n        MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferOutputStream, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE,\n                compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime, originalBatch.producerId(),\n                originalBatch.producerEpoch(), originalBatch.baseSequence(), originalBatch.isTransactional(),\n                originalBatch.isControlBatch(), originalBatch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), bufferOutputStream.limit(), deleteHorizonMs);\n\n        for (Record record : retainedRecords)\n            builder.append(record);\n\n        if (originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2)\n            // we must preserve the last offset from the initial batch in order to ensure that the\n            // last sequence number from the batch remains even after compaction. Otherwise, the producer\n            // could incorrectly see an out of sequence error.\n            builder.overrideLastOffset(originalBatch.lastOffset());\n\n        return builder;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get the byte buffer that backs this instance for reading.\n     *\n     * <p>A duplicate of the underlying buffer is returned so that the caller's position and\n     * limit changes do not affect this instance. The returned buffer shares the same backing\n     * array (or memory-mapped region) as this instance; modifications to the buffer's content\n     * will be visible through this instance.\n     *\n     * @return A duplicate of the backing {@link ByteBuffer}; never {@code null}\n     */\n    public ByteBuffer buffer() {\n        return buffer.duplicate();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return a zero-copy slice of this record set starting at the given byte position.\n     *\n     * <p>The returned {@code MemoryRecords} is backed by the same underlying bytes as this\n     * instance (no copy is made). The slice starts at {@code position} and contains at most\n     * {@code size} bytes, clamped to the available bytes between {@code position} and the end\n     * of this record set.\n     *\n     * <p>For correct batch iteration, {@code position} should be aligned to a batch boundary.\n     * Slicing at an arbitrary byte offset may result in an unparseable leading partial batch.\n     *\n     * @param position The byte offset within this record set at which the slice begins; must\n     *                 be non-negative and not greater than {@link #sizeInBytes()}\n     * @param size     The maximum number of bytes to include in the slice; must be non-negative\n     * @return A new {@code MemoryRecords} view over the specified region; never {@code null}\n     * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code position} or {@code size} is negative, or if\n     *                                  {@code position} exceeds {@link #sizeInBytes()}\n     */\n    @Override\n    public MemoryRecords slice(int position, int size) {\n        if (position < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid position: \" + position + \" in read from \" + this);\n        if (position > buffer.limit())\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Slice from position \" + position + \" exceeds end position of \" + this);\n        if (size < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid size: \" + size + \" in read from \" + this);\n\n        int availableBytes = Math.min(size, buffer.limit() - position);\n        // As of now, clients module support Java11 hence can't use ByteBuffer::slice(position, size) method.\n        // So we need to create a duplicate buffer and set the position and limit. Duplicate buffer\n        // is backed by original bytes hence not the content but only the relative position and limit\n        // are changed in the duplicate buffer. Once the position and limit are set, we can call the\n        // slice method to get the sliced buffer, which is a backed by the original buffer with the\n        // position reset to 0 and limit set to the size of the slice.\n        ByteBuffer slicedBuffer = buffer.duplicate();\n        slicedBuffer.position(position);\n        slicedBuffer.limit(position + availableBytes);\n        // Reset the position to 0 so that the sliced view has a relative position.\n        slicedBuffer = slicedBuffer.slice();\n\n        return readableRecords(slicedBuffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return an {@link Iterable} over the {@link MutableRecordBatch}es in this record set.\n     *\n     * <p>The iterable is backed by a fixed reference to {@link #batchIterator()} and can be\n     * iterated multiple times. Each iteration creates a new iterator that reads from a\n     * duplicate of the backing buffer, so concurrent iterations do not interfere with each\n     * other.\n     *\n     * @return An iterable over the mutable record batches; never {@code null}\n     */\n    @Override\n    public Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches() {\n        return batches;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"MemoryRecords(size=\" + sizeInBytes() +\n                \", buffer=\" + buffer +\n                \")\";\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        MemoryRecords that = (MemoryRecords) o;\n\n        return buffer.equals(that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer.hashCode();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * A predicate applied to each {@link RecordBatch} and {@link Record} during a\n     * {@link MemoryRecords#filterTo} pass. Implementations decide which batches and records to\n     * retain in the output.\n     *\n     * <p>The filter is first applied at the batch level via\n     * {@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)}. Only batches that are not immediately\n     * discarded ({@link BatchRetention#DELETE}) are then examined record by record via\n     * {@link #shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch, Record)}.\n     */\n    public abstract static class RecordFilter {\n        /** The current wall-clock time in milliseconds, used to evaluate time-based retention. */\n        public final long currentTime;\n        /** The configured delete-retention period in milliseconds. */\n        public final long deleteRetentionMs;\n\n        public RecordFilter(final long currentTime, final long deleteRetentionMs) {\n            this.currentTime = currentTime;\n            this.deleteRetentionMs = deleteRetentionMs;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Encapsulates the result of a batch-level retention check, combining the\n         * {@link BatchRetention} decision with a flag indicating whether the batch contains a\n         * marker for an empty transaction.\n         */\n        public static class BatchRetentionResult {\n            /** The retention decision for the batch. */\n            public final BatchRetention batchRetention;\n            /**\n             * {@code true} if the batch contains a control record that marks the end of an\n             * otherwise empty transaction; {@code false} otherwise.\n             */\n            public final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            public BatchRetentionResult(final BatchRetention batchRetention,\n                                        final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) {\n                this.batchRetention = batchRetention;\n                this.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            }\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Batch-level retention policy applied before individual records are examined.\n         */\n        public enum BatchRetention {\n            /** Discard the entire batch without inspecting its records. */\n            DELETE,\n            /** Retain the batch even if all of its records are filtered out. */\n            RETAIN_EMPTY,\n            /** Discard the batch if it becomes empty after record-level filtering. */\n            DELETE_EMPTY\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether the full batch can be discarded (i.e. whether we even need to\n         * check the records individually).\n         *\n         * @param batch The batch to evaluate; never {@code null}\n         * @return A {@link BatchRetentionResult} containing the retention decision and the\n         *         empty-transaction-marker flag; never {@code null}\n         */\n        protected abstract BatchRetentionResult checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch batch);\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether a record should be retained in the log. Note that {@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)}\n         * is used prior to checking individual record retention. Only records from batches which were not\n         * explicitly discarded with {@link BatchRetention#DELETE} will be considered.\n         *\n         * @param recordBatch The batch that contains the record; never {@code null}\n         * @param record      The record to evaluate; never {@code null}\n         * @return {@code true} if the record should be written to the output; {@code false} if\n         *         it should be dropped\n         */\n        protected abstract boolean shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch recordBatch, Record record);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Aggregated statistics and output buffer produced by a\n     * {@link MemoryRecords#filterTo(RecordFilter, ByteBuffer, BufferSupplier)} pass.\n     *\n     * <p>The output buffer may differ from the destination buffer passed to {@code filterTo} if\n     * the filtered output exceeded the destination buffer's capacity and a larger buffer had to\n     * be allocated (see KAFKA-5316). Callers should always use {@link #outputBuffer()} rather\n     * than the original destination buffer to access the filtered data.\n     */\n    public static class FilterResult {\n        private ByteBuffer outputBuffer;\n        private int messagesRead = 0;\n        // Note that `bytesRead` should contain only bytes from batches that have been processed, i.e. bytes from\n        // `messagesRead` and any discarded batches.\n        private int bytesRead = 0;\n        private int messagesRetained = 0;\n        private int bytesRetained = 0;\n        private long maxOffset = -1L;\n        private long maxTimestamp = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        private long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = -1L;\n\n        private FilterResult(ByteBuffer outputBuffer) {\n            this.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(MutableRecordBatch retainedBatch, int numMessagesInBatch, boolean headerOnly) {\n            int bytesRetained = headerOnly ? DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD : retainedBatch.sizeInBytes();\n            updateRetainedBatchMetadata(retainedBatch.maxTimestamp(), retainedBatch.lastOffset(),\n                    retainedBatch.lastOffset(), numMessagesInBatch, bytesRetained);\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset,\n                                                 int messagesRetained, int bytesRetained) {\n            validateBatchMetadata(maxTimestamp, shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, maxOffset);\n            if (maxTimestamp > this.maxTimestamp) {\n                this.maxTimestamp = maxTimestamp;\n                this.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n            }\n            this.maxOffset = Math.max(maxOffset, this.maxOffset);\n            this.messagesRetained += messagesRetained;\n            this.bytesRetained += bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        private void validateBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset) {\n            if (maxTimestamp != RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP && shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"shallowOffset undefined for maximum timestamp \" + maxTimestamp);\n            if (maxOffset < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"maxOffset undefined\");\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Return the buffer containing the filtered output.\n         *\n         * <p>This may be a different buffer than the one originally passed to\n         * {@link MemoryRecords#filterTo} if the output grew beyond the destination buffer's\n         * capacity and a new, larger buffer was allocated.\n         *\n         * @return The output buffer; never {@code null}\n         */\n        public ByteBuffer outputBuffer() {\n            return outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Return the total number of records read during the filter pass, including records\n         * that were discarded.\n         *\n         * @return The number of records read\n         */\n        public int messagesRead() {\n            return messagesRead;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Return the total number of bytes read during the filter pass, including bytes from\n         * batches that were entirely discarded.\n         *\n         * @return The number of bytes read\n         */\n        public int bytesRead() {\n            return bytesRead;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Return the number of records written to the output buffer.\n         *\n         * @return The number of retained records\n         */\n        public int messagesRetained() {\n            return messagesRetained;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Return the number of bytes written to the output buffer.\n         *\n         * @return The number of retained bytes\n         */\n        public int bytesRetained() {\n            return bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Return the maximum log offset among all retained records.\n         *\n         * @return The maximum retained offset, or {@code -1} if no records were retained\n         */\n        public long maxOffset() {\n            return maxOffset;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Return the maximum timestamp among all retained records.\n         *\n         * @return The maximum retained timestamp, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP} if no\n         *         records with a timestamp were retained\n         */\n        public long maxTimestamp() {\n            return maxTimestamp;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Return the batch-level (shallow) offset of the record with the maximum timestamp.\n         *\n         * @return The shallow offset of the maximum-timestamp record, or {@code -1} if no\n         *         records with a timestamp were retained\n         */\n        public long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp() {\n            return shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Wrap an existing {@link ByteBuffer} as a read-only {@code MemoryRecords} instance.\n     *\n     * <p>The buffer is not copied; the returned instance holds a direct reference to it. The\n     * buffer's limit determines the number of bytes that will be iterated. The buffer's\n     * position is not modified by this method.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer containing encoded record batch data; must not be {@code null}\n     * @return A new {@code MemoryRecords} backed by the given buffer; never {@code null}\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords readableRecords(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        return new MemoryRecords(buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for the current magic version using the given\n     * buffer, compression, timestamp type, and base offset.\n     *\n     * <p>This is a convenience overload that uses {@link RecordBatch#CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE} and\n     * no producer identity ({@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_ID}).\n     *\n     * @param buffer        The destination buffer for the encoded batch data; must not be\n     *                      {@code null}\n     * @param compression   The compression to apply to the record data; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type for the batch; must not be\n     *                      {@link TimestampType#NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE}\n     * @param baseOffset    The base offset of the first record in the batch\n     * @return A new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder}; never {@code null}\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset) {\n        return builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, timestampType, baseOffset);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for the current magic version with an explicit\n     * maximum size limit.\n     *\n     * <p>If {@code timestampType} is {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME}, the log-append\n     * time is set to the current wall-clock time at the moment this method is called.\n     *\n     * @param buffer        The destination buffer; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param compression   The compression codec; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param baseOffset    The base offset of the first record\n     * @param maxSize       The maximum number of bytes the builder is allowed to write\n     * @return A new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder}; never {@code null}\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               int maxSize) {\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = System.currentTimeMillis();\n\n        return new MemoryRecordsBuilder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, timestampType, baseOffset,\n            logAppendTime, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE,\n            false, false, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH, maxSize);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} with an explicit magic version and log-append time,\n     * without producer identity.\n     *\n     * @param buffer        The destination buffer; must not be {@code must not be {@code null}\n     * @param baseOffset    The base offset of the first record\n     * @param logAppendTime The log-append time in milliseconds, or\n     *                      {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP} if not applicable\n     * @return A new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder}; never {@code null}\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} with an explicit magic version, without producer\n     * identity.\n     *\n     * <p>If {@code RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} with an explicit magic version, log-append time,\n     * and partition leader epoch, without                          Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime,\n                                               int partitionLeaderEpoch) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH,\n                false, records);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Build a {@code MemoryRecords} containing the given records in a single batch with full\n     * control over all batch-level parameters.\n     *\n     * <p>If {@code records} is empty, {@link #EMPTY} is returned immediately without\n     * allocating a buffer.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance note:</b> The buffer size is estimated before encoding begins. If the\n     * estimate is too small (e.g., due to compression expanding the data), the underlying\n     * {@link ByteBufferOutputStream} will reallocate and copy. For predictable workloads,\n     * pre-sizing the buffer via a {@link #builder} overload avoids this reallocation.\n     *\n     * @param magic                The record format version (magic byte)\n     * @param initialOffset        The base offset of the first record\n     * @param compression          The compression codec; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param timestampType        The timestamp type; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param producerId           The producer id, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_ID} if none\n     * @param producerEpoch        The producer epoch, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH}\n     *                             if none\n     * @param baseSequence         The base sequence number, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_SEQUENCE}\n     *                             if none\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch, or\n     *                             {@link RecordBatch#NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH} if unknown\n     * @param isTransactional      {@code true} if the batch belongs to a transaction\n     * @param records              The records to include; must not be {@code null}\n     * @return A new {@code MemoryRecords}, or {@link #EMPTY} if {@code records} is empty;\n     *         never {@code null}\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withRecords(byte magic, long initialOffset, Compression compression,\n                                            TimestampType timestampType, long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                            int baseSequence, int partitionLeaderEpoch, boolean isTransactional,\n                                            SimpleRecord... records) {\n        if (records.length == 0)\n            return MemoryRecords.EMPTY;\n        int sizeEstimate = AbstractRecords.estimateSizeInBytes(magic, compression.type(), Arrays.asList(records));\n        ByteBufferOutputStream bufferStream = new ByteBufferOutputStream(sizeEstimate);\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = System.currentTimeMillis();\n        try (final MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferStream, magic, compression, timestampType,\n                initialOffset, logAppendTime, producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, false,\n                partitionLeaderEpoch, sizeEstimate)) {\n            for (SimpleRecord record : records)\n                builder.append(record);\n            return builder.build();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Build a {@code MemoryRecords} containing a single end-of-transaction control batch at\n     * base offset 0 and the current wall-clock time.\n     *\n     * <p>End-of-transaction markers are control records that signal the commit or abort of a\n     * transaction to consumers. They are written by the broker's transaction coordinator.\n     *\n     * @param producerId    The producer id of the transactional producer\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch\n     * @param marker        The end-of-transaction marker to encode; must not be {@code null}\n     * @return A new {@code MemoryRecords} containing the control batch; never {@code null}\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withEndTransactionMarker(long producerId, short producerEpoch, EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        return withEndTransactionMarker(0L, System.currentTimeMillis(), RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH,\n                producerId, producerEpoch, marker);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Build a {@code MemoryRecords} containing a single end-of-transaction control batch at\n     * base offset 0 and the specified timestamp.\n     *\n     * @param timestamp     The timestamp to assign to the control record, in milliseconds since\n     *                      the Unix epoch\n     * @param producerId    The producer id of the transactional producer\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch\n     * @param marker        The end-of-transaction marker to encode; must not be {@code null}\n     * @return A new {@code MemoryRecords} containing the control batch; never {@code null}\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withEndTransactionMarker(long timestamp, long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                                         EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        return withEndTransactionMarker(0L, timestamp, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH, producerId,\n                producerEpoch, marker);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Build a {@code MemoryRecords} containing a single end-of-transaction control batch with\n     * full control over all batch-level parameters.\n     *\n     * @param initialOffset        The base offset of the control batch\n     * @param timestamp            The timestamp to assign to the control record, in milliseconds\n     *                             since the Unix epoch\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param producerId           The producer id of the transactional producer\n     * @param producerEpoch        The producer epoch\n     * @param marker               The end-of-transaction marker to encode; must not be\n     *                             {@code null}\n     * @return A new {@code MemoryRecords} containing the control batch; never {@code null}\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withEndTransactionMarker(long initialOffset, long timestamp, int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                                         long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                                         EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        int endTxnMarkerBatchSize = DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD + marker.endTxnMarkerValueSize();\n        ByteBuffer buffer = ByteBuffer.allocate(endTxnMarkerBatchSize);\n        writeEndTransactionalMarker(buffer, initialOffset, timestamp, partitionLeaderEpoch, producerId,\n                producerEpoch, marker);\n        buffer.flip();\n        return MemoryRecords.readableRecords(buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Encode a single end-of-transaction control batch directly into the given buffer.\n     *\n     * <p>Unlike {@link #withEndTransactionMarker}, this method writes into a caller-supplied\n     * buffer rather than allocating a new one. The buffer's position is advanced past the\n     * written bytes. The buffer must have sufficient remaining capacity to hold the encoded\n     * batch.\n     *\n     * @param buffer               The destination buffer; must not be {@code null} and must\n     *                             have sufficient remaining capacity\n     * @param initialOffset        The base offset of the control batch\n     * @param timestamp            The timestamp to assign to the control record, in milliseconds\n     *                             since the Unix epoch\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param producerId           The producer id of the transactional producer\n     * @param producerEpoch        The producer epoch\n     * @param marker               The end-of-transaction marker to encode; must not be\n     *                             {@code null}\n     */\n    public static void writeEndTransactionalMarker(ByteBuffer buffer, long initialOffset, long timestamp,\n                                                   int partitionLeaderEpoch, long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                                   EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        boolean isTransactional = true;\n        try (MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, Compression.NONE,\n                TimestampType.CREATE_TIME, initialOffset, timestamp, producerId, producerEpoch,\n                RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, isTransactional, true, partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                buffer.capacity())\n        ) {\n            builder.appendEndTxnMarker(timestamp, marker);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Build a {@code MemoryRecords} containing a single KRaft control batch with a\n     * {@link LeaderChangeMessage} record.\n     *\n     * <p>Leader-change messages are KRaft control records written to the {@code __cluster_metadata}\n     * topic when a new partition leader is elected.\n     *\n     * @param initialOffset       The base offset of the control batch\n     * @param timestamp           The timestamp to assign to the control record, in milliseconds\n     *                            since the Unix epoch\n     * @param leaderEpoch         The partition leader epoch\n     * @param buffer              The destination buffer; must not be {@code null} and must have\n     *                            sufficient remaining capacity\n     * @param leaderChangeMessage The leader-change message to encode; must not be {@code null}\n     * @return A new {@code MemoryRecords} containing the control batch; never {@code null}\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withLeaderChangeMessage(\n        long initialOffset,\n        long timestamp,\n        int leaderEpoch,\n        ByteBuffer buffer,\n        LeaderChangeMessage leaderChangeMessage\n    ) {\n        try (MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = createKraftControlRecordBuilder(\n                initialOffset,\n                timestamp,\n                leaderEpoch,\n                buffer\n            )\n        ) {\n            builder.appendLeaderChangeMessage(timestamp, leaderChangeMessage);\n            return builder.build();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Build a {@code MemoryRecords} containing a single KRaft control batch with a\n     * {@link SnapshotHeaderRecord}.\n     *\n     * <p>Snapshot header records mark the beginning of a KRaft snapshot and are written to the\n     * {@code __cluster_metadata} topic.\n     *\n     * @param initialOffset        The base offset of the control batch\n     * @param timestamp            The timestamp to assign to the control record, in milliseconds\n     *                             since the Unix epoch\n     * @param leaderEpoch          The partition leader epoch\n     * @param buffer               The destination buffer; never {@code null}\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withSnapshotHeaderRecord(\n        long initialOffset,\n        long timestamp,\n        int leaderEpoch,\n        ByteBuffer buffer,\n        SnapshotHeaderRecord snapshotHeaderRecord\n    ) {\n        try (MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = createKraftControlRecordBuilder(\n                initialOffset,\n                timestamp,\n                leaderEpoch,\n                buffer\n            )\n        ) {\n            builder.appendSnapshotHeaderMessage(timestamp, snapshotHeaderRecord);\n            return builder.build();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Build a {@code MemoryRecords} containing a single KRaft control batch with a\n     * {@link SnapshotFooterRecord}.\n     *\n     * <p>Snapshot footer records mark the end of a KRaft snapshot and are written to the\n     * {@code __cluster_metadata} topic.\n     *\n     * @param initialOffset        The base offset of the control batch\n     * @param timestamp            The timestamp to assign to the control record, in milliseconds\n     *                             since the Unix epoch\n     * @param leaderEpoch          The partition leader epoch\n     * @param buffer               The destination buffer;
